items-center gap-2" id="introduction"><a data-card="" href="#introduction" class="peer">Introduction</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>This guide shows you how to use Prisma with Next.js, a fullstack React framework. You&#x27;ll learn how to create a <a href="/docs/postgres">Prisma Postgres</a> instance, set up Prisma ORM with Next.js, handle migrations, and deploy your application to Vercel.</p>
<p>You can find a <a href="https://github.com/prisma/prisma-examples/blob/latest/orm/nextjs" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">deployment-ready example on GitHub</a>.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="prerequisites"><a data-card="" href="#prerequisites" class="peer">Prerequisites</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://nodejs.org" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Node.js</a> v20.19+, v22.12+, or v24.0+</li>
<li>A Vercel account (if you want to deploy your application)</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="1-set-up-your-project"><a data-card="" href="#1-set-up-your-project" class="peer">1. Set up your project</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>From the directory where you want to create your project, run <code>create-next-app</code> to create a new Next.js app that you will be using for this guide.</p>

<p>You will be prompted to answer a few questions about your project. Select all of the defaults.</p>
<div role="alert" class="relative w-full rounded-md border p-4 gap-3 text-sm [&amp;&gt;svg]:left-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:top-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:w-5 [&amp;&gt;svg]:h-5 alert-admonition flex items-start [&amp;&gt;i]:mt-0.5 bg-background-ppg text-foreground-ppg border-none [&amp;&gt;svg]:text-foreground-ppg"><i class="fa-duotone fa-solid fa-circle-exclamation"></i><div class="[&amp;&gt;*]:first:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;*]:last:mb-0 [&amp; strong]:text-inherit"><p>For reference, those are:</p><ul>
<li>TypeScript</li>
<li>ESLint</li>
<li>Tailwind CSS</li>
<li>No <code>src</code> directory</li>
<li>App Router</li>
<li>Turbopack</li>
<li>No customized import alias</li>
</ul></div></div>
<p>Then, navigate to the project directory:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">cd</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> nextjs-prisma</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="2-install-and-configure-prisma"><a data-card="" href="#2-install-and-configure-prisma" class="peer">2. Install and Configure Prisma</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="21-install-dependencies"><a data-card="" href="#21-install-dependencies" class="peer">2.1. Install dependencies</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>To get started with Prisma, you&#x27;ll need to install a few dependencies:</p>

<div role="alert" class="relative w-full rounded-md border p-4 gap-3 text-sm [&amp;&gt;svg]:left-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:top-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:w-5 [&amp;&gt;svg]:h-5 alert-admonition flex items-start [&amp;&gt;i]:mt-0.5 bg-background-ppg text-foreground-ppg border-none [&amp;&gt;svg]:text-foreground-ppg"><i class="fa-duotone fa-solid fa-circle-exclamation"></i><div class="[&amp;&gt;*]:first:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;*]:last:mb-0 [&amp; strong]:text-inherit"><p>If you are using a different database provider (MySQL, SQL Server, SQLite), install the corresponding driver adapter package instead of <code>@prisma/adapter-pg</code>. For more information, see <a href="/docs/orm/core-concepts/supported-databases/database-drivers">Database drivers</a>.</p></div></div>
<p>Once installed, initialize Prisma in your project:</p>

role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="radix-_R_jp7lfivpfiv9db_-trigger-bun" hidden="" id="radix-_R_jp7lfivpfiv9db_-content-bun" tabindex="0"></div></div>
<div role="alert" class="relative w-full rounded-md border p-4 gap-3 text-sm [&amp;&gt;svg]:left-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:top-4 [&amp;&gt;svg]:w-5 [&amp;&gt;svg]:h-5 alert-admonition flex items-start [&amp;&gt;i]:mt-0.5 bg-background-ppg text-foreground-ppg border-none [&amp;&gt;svg]:text-foreground-ppg"><i class="fa-duotone fa-solid fa-circle-exclamation"></i><div class="[&amp;&gt;*]:first:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;*]:last:mb-0 [&amp; strong]:text-inherit"><p>You&#x27;ll need to answer a few questions while setting up your Prisma Postgres database. Select the region closest to your location and a memorable name for your database like &quot;My *<strong>*__**</strong> Project&quot;</p></div></div>
<p>This will create:</p>
<ul>
<li>A <code>prisma</code> directory with a <code>schema.prisma</code> file.</li>
<li>A <code>prisma.config.ts</code> file for configuring Prisma.</li>
<li>A Prisma Postgres database.</li>
<li>A <code>.env</code> file containing the <code>DATABASE_URL</code> at the project root.</li>
</ul>
<p>The <code>app/generated/prisma</code> output directory for the generated Prisma Client will be created when you run <code>prisma generate</code> or <code>prisma migrate dev</code> in a later step.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="22-define-your-prisma-schema"><a data-card="" href="#22-define-your-prisma-schema" class="peer">2.2. Define your Prisma Schema</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>In the <code>prisma/schema.prisma</code> file, add the following models:</p>

1.0091.0158 1.4555l4.3759 6.7786c.2608.4046.7127.6388 1.1823.6388.1332 0 .267-.0188.3987-.0577l12.7019-3.7568c.3891-.1151.7072-.3904.8737-.7553s.1633-.7828-.0075-1.1454zm-1.8481.7519L9.1814 <span class="line diff add"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">} </span></span>
<span class="line diff add"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Post</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { </span></span>
<span class="line diff add"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id        </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">     @id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">autoincrement</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()) </span></span>
<span class="line diff add"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  title     </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span></span>
<span class="line diff add"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  content   </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">String</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">?</span></span>
<span class="line diff add"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  published </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Boolean</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> @default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">false</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span></span>
<span class="line diff add"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  authorId  </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Int</span></span>
<span class="line diff add"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  author    </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">User</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">    @relation</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">fields</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: [</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">authorId</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">], </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">references</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: [</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">]) </span></span>
<span class="line diff add"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">} </span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>This creates two models: <code>User</code> and <code>Post</code>, with a one-to-many relationship between them.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="23-add-dotenv-to-prismaconfigts"><a data-card="" href="#23-add-dotenv-to-prismaconfigts" class="peer">2.3 Add <code>dotenv</code> to <code>prisma.config.ts</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>To get access to the variables in the <code>.env</code> file, they can either be loaded by your runtime, or by using <code>dotenv</code>.
Include an import for <code>dotenv</code> at the top of the <code>prisma.config.ts</code></p>

<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="24-run-migrations-and-generate-prisma-client"><a data-card="" href="#24-run-migrations-and-generate-prisma-client" class="peer">2.4. <h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="25-seed-the-database"><a data-card="" href="#25-seed-the-database" class="peer">2.5. Seed the database</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Add some seed data to populate the database with sample users and posts.</p>
<p>Create a new file called <code>seed.ts</code> in the <code>prisma/</code> directory:</p>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>Finally, run <code>prisma db seed</code> to seed your database with the initial data we defined in the <code>seed.ts</code> file.</p>
<p>Run the seed script:</p>

<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="26-set-up-prisma-client"><a data-card="" href="#26-set-up-prisma-client" class="peer">2.6 Set up Prisma Client</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Now that you have a database with some initial data, you can set up Prisma Client and connect it to your database.</p>
<p>At the root of your project, create a new <code>lib</code> directory and add a <code>prisma.ts</code> file to it.</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">mkdir</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> -p</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> lib</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &amp;&amp; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">touch</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> lib/prisma.ts</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>

<span class="line diff add"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">if</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (process.env.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">NODE_ENV</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> !==</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;production&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) globalForPrisma.prisma </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prisma; </span></span>
<span class="line diff add"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">export</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prisma; </span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>This file creates a Prisma Client and attaches it to the global object so that only one instance of the client is created in your application. This helps resolve issues with hot reloading that can occur when using Prisma ORM with Next.js in development mode.</p>
<p>You&#x27;ll use this client in the next section to run your first queries.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="3-query-your-database-with-prisma-orm"><a data-card="" href="#3-query-your-database-with-prisma-orm" class="peer">3. Query your database with Prisma ORM</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Now that you have an initialized Prisma Client, a connection to your database, and some initial data, you can start querying your data with Prisma ORM.</p>
<p>In this example, you&#x27;ll make the &quot;home&quot; page of your application display all of your users.</p>
<p>Open the <code>app/page.tsx</code> file and replace the existing code with the following:</p>

<p>This gives you a basic page with a title and a list of users. However, that list is static with hardcoded values. Let&#x27;s update the page to fetch the users from your database and make it dynamic.</p>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">div</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> className</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;min-h-screen bg-gray-50 flex flex-col items-center justify-center -mt-16&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">h1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> className</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;text-4xl font-bold mb-8 font-[family-name:var(--font-geist-sans)] text-[#333333]&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        Superblog</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">h1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">ol</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> className</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;list-decimal list-inside font-[family-name:var(--font-geist-sans)]&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        {users.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">map</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">((</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">user</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">          &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">li</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> key</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">{user.id} </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">className</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;mb-2&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">            {user.name}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">          &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">li</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        ))}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">ol</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">div</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  );</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>You are now importing your client, querying the <code>User</code> model for all users, and then displaying them in a list.</p>
<p>Now your home page is dynamic and will display the users from your database.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="31-update-your-data-optional"><a data-card="" href="#31-update-your-data-optional" class="peer">3.1 Update your data (optional)</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>If you want to see what happens when data is updated, you could:</p>
<ul>
<li>update your <code>User</code> table via a SQL browser of your choice</li>
<li>change your <code>seed.ts</code> file to add more users</li>
<li>change the call to <code>prisma.user.findMany</code> to re-order the users, filter the users, or similar.</li>
</ul>
<p>Just reload the page and you&#x27;ll see the changes.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="4-add-a-new-posts-list-page"><a data-card="" href="#4-add-a-new-posts-list-page" class="peer">4. Add a new Posts list page</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>You have your home page working, but you should add a new page that displays all of your posts.</p>
<p>First create a new <code>posts</code> directory in the <code>app</code> directory and create a new <code>page.tsx</code> file inside of it.</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">mkdir</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> -p</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> app/posts</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &amp;&amp; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">touch</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> app/posts/page.tsx</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>Second, add the following code to the <code>app/posts/page.tsx</code> file:</p>

<p>Now <code>localhost:3000/posts</code> will load, but the content is hardcoded again. Let&#x27;s update it to be dynamic, similarly to the home page:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" <span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">div</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> className</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;min-h-screen bg-gray-50 flex flex-col items-center justify-center -mt-16 text-[#333333]&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>

<p>This works similarly to the home page, but instead of displaying users, it displays posts. You can also see that you&#x27;ve used <code>include</code> in your Prisma Client query to fetch the author of each post so you can display the author&#x27;s name.</p>
<p>This &quot;list view&quot; is one of the most common patterns in web applications. You&#x27;re going to add two more pages to your application which you&#x27;ll also commonly need: a &quot;detail view&quot; and a &quot;create view&quot;.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="5-add-a-new-posts-detail-page"><a data-card="" href="#5-add-a-new-posts-detail-page" class="peer">5. Add a new Posts detail page</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>To complement the Posts list page, you&#x27;ll add a Posts detail page.</p>
<p>In the <code>posts</code> directory, create a new <code>[id]</code> directory and a new <code>page.tsx</code> file inside of that.</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">mkdir</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> -p</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;app/posts/[id]&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &amp;&amp; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">touch</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;app/posts/[id]/page.tsx&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>This page will display a single post&#x27;s title, content, and author. Just like your other pages, add the following code to the <code>app/posts/new/page.tsx</code> file:</p>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">div</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> className</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;prose prose-gray mt-8&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;{post.content </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">||</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;No content available.&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}&lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">div</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">article</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">div</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  );</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>There&#x27;s a lot of changes here, so let&#x27;s break it down:</p>
<ul>
<li>You&#x27;re using Prisma Client to fetch the post by its <code>id</code>, which you get from the <code>params</code> object.</li>
<li>In case the post doesn&#x27;t exist (maybe it was deleted or maybe you typed a wrong ID), you call <code>notFound()</code> to display a 404 page.</li>
<li>You then display the post&#x27;s title, content, and author. If the post doesn&#x27;t have content, you display a placeholder message.</li>
</ul>
<p>It&#x27;s not the prettiest page, but it&#x27;s a good start. Try it out by navigating to <code>localhost:3000/posts/1</code> and <code>localhost:3000/posts/2</code>. You can also test the 404 page by navigating to <code>localhost:3000/posts/999</code>.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="6-add-a-new-posts-create-page"><a data-card="" href="#6-add-a-new-posts-create-page" class="peer">6. Add a new Posts create page</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>To round out your application, you&#x27;ll add a &quot;create&quot; page for posts. This will let you write your own posts and save them to the database.</p>
<p>As with the other pages, you&#x27;ll start with a static page and then update it to be dynamic.</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">mkdir</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> -p</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> app/posts/new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> &amp;&amp; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">touch</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> app/posts/new/page.tsx</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>Now, add the following code to the <code>app/posts/new/page.tsx</code> file:</p>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">          /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">div</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">          &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">label</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> htmlFor</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;content&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> className</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;block text-lg mb-2&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">            Content</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">          &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">label</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> htmlFor</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;title&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> className</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;block text-lg mb-2&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">            Title</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">          &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">label</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">          &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">input</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">            type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;text&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">            id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;title&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">            name</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;title&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">            placeholder</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Enter your post title&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">            className</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;w-full px-4 py-2 border rounded-lg&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">          /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">div</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">div</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">          &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">label</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> htmlFor</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;content&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> className</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;block text-lg mb-2&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">            Content</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">          &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">label</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">          &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">textarea</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">            id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;content&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">            name</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;content&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">            placeholder</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Write your post content here...&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">            rows</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">{</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">6</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">            className</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;w-full px-4 py-2 border rounded-lg&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">          /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">div</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">button</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">          type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;submit&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">          className</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;w-full bg-blue-500 text-white py-3 rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-600&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        &gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">          Create Post</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">button</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">Form</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">div</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  );</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>This page now has a functional form! When you submit the form, it will create a new post in the database and redirect you to the posts list page.</p>
<p>You also added a <code>revalidatePath</code> call to revalidate the posts list page so that it will be updated with the new post. That way everyone can read the new post immediately.</p>
<p>Try it out by navigating to <code>localhost:3000/posts/new</code> and submitting the form.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="7-deploy-your-application-to-vercel-optional"><a data-card="" href="#7-deploy-your-application-to-vercel-optional" class="peer">7. Deploy your application to Vercel (Optional)</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>The quickest way to deploy your application to Vercel is to use the <a href="https://vercel.com/docs/cli" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Vercel CLI</a>.</p>
<p>First, install the Vercel CLI:</p>

tabindex="0"></div></div>
<p>Then, run <code>vercel login</code> to log in to your Vercel account.</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">vercel</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> login</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>Before you deploy, you also need to tell Vercel to make sure that the Prisma Client is generated. You can do this by adding a <code>postinstall</code> script to your <code>package.json</code> file.</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex text-fd-muted-foreground items-center gap-2 h-9.5 border-b px-4"><div class="[&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M 6,1 C 4.354992,1 3,2.354992 3,4 v 16 c 0,1.645008 1.354992,3 3,3 h 12 c 1.645008,0 3,-1.354992 3,-3 V 8 7 A 1.0001,1.0001 0 0 0 20.707031,6.2929687 l -5,-5 A 1.0001,1.0001 0 0 0 15,1 h -1 z m 0,2 h 7 v 3 c 0,1.645008 1.354992,3 3,3 h 3 v 11 c 0,0.564129 -0.435871,1 -1,1 H 6 C 5.4358712,21 5,20.564129 5,20 V 4 C 5,3.4358712 5.4358712,3 6,3 Z M 15,3.4140625 18.585937,7 H 16 C 15.435871,7 15,6.5641288 15,6 Z" fill="currentColor" /></svg></div><figcaption class="flex-1 truncate">package.json</figcaption><div class="empty:hidden -me-2"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">{</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  &quot;name&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;nextjs-prisma&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  &quot;version&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;0.1.0&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  &quot;private&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">true</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  &quot;scripts&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;dev&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;next dev --turbopack&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;build&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;next build&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;postinstall&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;prisma generate&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;start&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;next start&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;lint&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;next lint&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  &quot;prisma&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;seed&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;tsx prisma/seed.ts&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  &quot;dependencies&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;@prisma/adapter-pg&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;^6.2.1&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;@prisma/client&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;^6.2.1&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;next&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;15.1.4&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;pg&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;^8.13.1&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;react&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;^19.0.0&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;react-dom&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;^19.0.0&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  &quot;devDependencies&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;@eslint/eslintrc&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;^3&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;@types/node&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;^20&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;@types/react&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;^19&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;@types/react-dom&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;^19&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;eslint&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;^9&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;eslint-config-next&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;15.1.4&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;postcss&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;^8&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;prisma&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;^6.2.1&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;tailwindcss&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;^3.4.1&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;tsx&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;^4.19.2&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;typescript&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;^5&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>After this change, you can deploy your application to Vercel by running <code>vercel</code>.</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">vercel</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>After the deployment is complete, you can visit your application at the URL that Vercel provides. Congratulations, you&#x27;ve just deployed a Next.js application with Prisma ORM!</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="8-next-steps"><a data-card="" href="#8-next-steps" class="peer">8. Next steps</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Now that you have a working Next.js application with Prisma ORM, here are some ways you can expand and improve your application:</p>
<ul>
<li>Add authentication to protect your routes</li>
<li>Add the ability to edit and delete posts</li>
<li>Add comments to posts</li>
<li>Use <a href="/docs/studio">Prisma Studio</a> for visual database management</li>
</ul>
<p>For more information:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/docs/orm">Prisma ORM documentation</a></li>
<li><a href="/docs/orm/prisma-client/setup-and-configuration/introduction">Prisma Client API reference</a></li>
<li><a href="https://nextjs.org/docs" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Next.js documentation</a></li>

v7)\n\n\u003e **Note**: This guide is updated for **Prisma ORM 7**. Key changes from earlier versions:\n\u003e\n\u003e - `engine` property removed from `prisma.config.ts`\n\u003e - `url` removed from datasource in `schema.prisma` (now only in `prisma.config.ts`)\n\u003e - Use `@prisma/adapter-pg` driver adapter for direct TCP connections\n\u003e - `--no-engine` flag is no longer required for `prisma generate`\n\u003e - Requires Node.js 20.19+ and TypeScript 5.4.0+\n\n## Overview of implementing Prisma with Next.js\n\n1. Install Prisma and required dependencies (including dotenv)\n2. Initialize Prisma and configure schema\n3. Configure dotenv for environment variables\n4. IT WILL BREAK THE APPLICATION\ngenerator client {\n  provider = \"prisma-client-js\"     // ❌ BREAKS APPLICATION\n}\n\n// ❌ NEVER USE default import location - IT WILL BREAK THE APPLICATION\nimport { PrismaClient } from '@prisma/client'  // ❌ BREAKS APPLICATION\n\n// ❌ WRONG IMPORT PATH - You MUST use `provider = \"prisma-client\"` (not \"prisma-client-js\")\n2. You MUST use custom output: `output = \"../app/generated/prisma\"`\n3. You MUST use `@prisma/adapter-pg` driver adapter\n4. You MUST create `lib/prisma.ts` as a global singleton instance\n5. You MUST wrap all database calls in try-catch blocks\n6. Do NOT attempt to run this command yourself.\n\n```bash\n# Initialize Prisma AND create a real Prisma Postgres cloud database\nnpx prisma init --db --output ../app/generated/prisma\n```\n\nThis command:\n\n- Authenticates you with Prisma Console (if needed)\n- Prompts for **region** and **project name**\n- **Creates a cloud Prisma Postgres database**\n- Generates:\n  - `prisma/schema.prisma` (with correct output path)\n  - `prisma.config.ts` (with dotenv import)\n  - **`.env` with a `DATABASE_URL`**\n\n**IMPORTANT**: Ensure the generated `.env` uses a `postgres://` URL scheme.
